The described changes\\n25: // are not applied directly, but contain an approximation of the final\\n26: // result that will be completed during apply by resolving any values that\\n27: // cannot be predicted.\\n28: //\\n29: // A plan must always be accompanied by the configuration it was built from,\\n30: // since the plan does not itself include all of the information required to\\n31: // make the changes indicated.\\n32: type Plan struct {\\n33: \\t// Mode is the mode under which this plan was created.\\n34: \\t//\\n35: \\t// This is only recorded to allow for UI differences when presenting plans\\n36: \\t// to the end-user, and so it must not be used to influence apply-time\\n37: \\t// behavior. VariableValues can potentially contain\\n53: \\t// unknown values for a speculative plan, but the variable values must\\n54: \\t// all be known for a plan that will subsequently be applied.\\n55: \\t//\\n56: \\t// ApplyTimeVariables retains the names of any ephemeral variables that were\\n57: \\t// set (non-null) during the planning phase and must therefore be\\n58: \\t// re-supplied by the caller (potentially with different values) during\\n59: \\t// the apply phase. Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/terraform\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of the planned changes grouped by action type.\n// The output shows one line per resource change in the format:\n//   [action] resource_type.name\n// followed by a summary count at the end.\nfunc (c *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Only include non-NoOp changes\n\t\tif rc.Action != plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tactionGroups[rc.Action] = append(actionGroups[rc.Action], rc)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order to display actions\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Track total counts\n\ttotalCounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\n\t// Print changes grouped by action in the defined order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort changes by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print each change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceAddr := formatResourceAddress(rc.Addr)\n\t\t\tsymbol := getActionSymbol(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\\n\", symbol, resourceAddr))\n\t\t\ttotalCounts[action]++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tif len(totalCounts) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\t\tcount := totalCounts[action]\n\t\t\tif count > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tlabel := getActionLabel(action)\n\t\t\t\tplural := buf.String()\n}\n\n// formatResourceAddress returns a string representation of a resource instance address\n// in the format \"type.name\" or \"data.type.name\" for data sources.\nfunc actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort changes by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print each change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceAddr := formatResourceAddress(rc.Addr)\n\t\t\tsymbol := getActionSymbol(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\\n\", symbol, resourceAddr))\n\t\t\ttotalCounts[action]++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tif len(totalCounts) > 0 \"\"\n\t\t\t\tif count != 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\tplural = \"s\"\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %d %s%s\\n\", label, count, noun(action), plural))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// formatResourceAddress returns a string representation of a resource instance address\n// in the format \"type.name\" or \"data.type.name\" for data sources.\nfunc formatResourceAddress(addr addrs.AbsResourceInstance) string {\n\tresource := addr.Resource.Resource\n\tmodule := addr.Module\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Include module path if not root\n\tif !module.IsRoot() {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(module.String())\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\".\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Add resource prefix for data sources\n\tif resource.Mode == addrs.DataResourceMode {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"data.\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Add type and name\n\tbuf.WriteString(resource.Type)\n\tbuf.WriteString(\".\")\n\tbuf.WriteString(resource.Name)\n\n\t// Add instance key if present\n\tif addr.InstanceKey != nil {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"[\")\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(addr.InstanceKey.String())\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"]\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// getActionSymbol returns a short symbol for the action.\nfunc getActionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"[+]\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"[~]\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"[-]\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"[-/+]\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"[+/-]\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"[<=]\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"[.]\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"[+/.]\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"[?]\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// getActionLabel returns a human-readable label for the action.\nfunc getActionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Create then forget\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// noun returns the singular noun for a resource action.\nfunc noun(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.Read, plans.Delete, plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"resource\"\n\tcase plans.Update, plans.DeleteThenCreate, plans.CreateThenDelete, plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"resource\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"resource\"\n\t}\n}\n","numLines":189,"startLine":1,"totalLines":189}}}
